\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{sentence\PYZus{}transformers} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{SentenceTransformer}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{numpy} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{np}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{textwrap}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{torch}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. GPU\PYZhy{}Accelerated Embeddings}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Loading Retriever...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{SentenceTransformer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{all\PYZhy{}MiniLM\PYZhy{}L6\PYZhy{}v2}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{device}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Our tiny mock Knowledge Base (Vector DB)}
\PY{n}{kb} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}
    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Hugging Face Transformers is a library for state\PYZhy{}of\PYZhy{}the\PYZhy{}art NLP.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Retrieval\PYZhy{}Augmented Generation helps reduce hallucinations by grounding LLMs on retrieved documents.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Perplexity is the exponentiated average negative log\PYZhy{}likelihood.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Cross\PYZhy{}entropy between true distribution p and model q is H(p,q) = \PYZhy{}Σ p(x) log q(x).}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{kb\PYZus{}embs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{kb}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{convert\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}numpy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normalize\PYZus{}embeddings}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{retrieve\PYZus{}top\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{k}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{q\PYZus{}emb} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{convert\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}numpy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normalize\PYZus{}embeddings}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Dot product similarity (because vectors are L2\PYZhy{}normalized, this equals Cosine Similarity)}
    \PY{n}{scores} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{kb\PYZus{}embs} \PY{o}{@} \PY{n}{q\PYZus{}emb}
    \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argsort}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{k}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{kb}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. Load Generator (Natively in bfloat16 \PYZhy{} No bitsandbytes needed!)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Loading Generator (bfloat16)...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{transformers} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{AutoTokenizer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Using a modern instruction\PYZhy{}tuned model}
\PY{n}{gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{google/gemma\PYZhy{}2\PYZhy{}2b\PYZhy{}it}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} We just use torch\PYZus{}dtype=torch.bfloat16. Simple, fast, stable.}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}gen} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{,} 
    \PY{n}{torch\PYZus{}dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bfloat16}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{device\PYZus{}map}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{auto}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Automatically puts it on your RTX 3090}
\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. RAG Pipeline}
\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{rag\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step A: Retrieve relevant documents based on semantic similarity}
    \PY{n}{hits} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{retrieve\PYZus{}top\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{k}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{context} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{} }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{txt}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{txt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{hits}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step B: Construct a prompt forcing the LLM to use ONLY the context}
    \PY{n}{prompt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{textwrap}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dedent}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}}
\PY{l+s+s2}{    Answer the question based only on the provided context.}
\PY{l+s+s2}{    }
\PY{l+s+s2}{    Context:}
\PY{l+s+s2}{    }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{context}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}
\PY{l+s+s2}{    }
\PY{l+s+s2}{    Question: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{query}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}
\PY{l+s+s2}{    }
\PY{l+s+s2}{    Answer:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{n}{inputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{prompt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{return\PYZus{}tensors}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{pt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step C: Generate the answer}
    \PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{outputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{generate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{inputs}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}new\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{temperature}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}\PY{p}{)}
        
    \PY{n}{answer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{outputs}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{skip\PYZus{}special\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{answer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Answer:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} RAG Inference \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Q: How is RAG useful?}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{A:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{How is RAG useful?}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{Q: What is the math behind Perplexity?}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{A:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{What is the math behind Perplexity?}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
A: RAG helps reduce hallucinations by grounding LLMs on retrieved documents.

Q: What is the math behind Perplexity?
A: Perplexity is the exponentiated average negative log-likelihood.

    \hypertarget{rag-for-myanmar-language}{%
\subsection{RAG for Myanmar Language}\label{rag-for-myanmar-language}}

{\burmesefont ဒီတခါတော့} {\burmesefont မြန်မာစာနဲ့} RAG {\burmesefont ကို} {\burmesefont ဆောက်ပြပြီး} {\burmesefont မေးခွန်းမေးကြည့်ကြရအောင်။}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. THE MULTILINGUAL RETRIEVER}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Loading Multilingual Retriever...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} We MUST use a multilingual model here. English\PYZhy{}only MiniLM will fail on Myanmar.}
\PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{SentenceTransformer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{paraphrase\PYZhy{}multilingual\PYZhy{}MiniLM\PYZhy{}L12\PYZhy{}v2}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{device}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Embedding Knowledge Base...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{kb\PYZus{}embs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{bbc\PYZus{}paragraphs}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{convert\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}numpy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normalize\PYZus{}embeddings}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{retrieve\PYZus{}top\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{k}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{q\PYZus{}emb} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{convert\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}numpy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normalize\PYZus{}embeddings}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{scores} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{kb\PYZus{}embs} \PY{o}{@} \PY{n}{q\PYZus{}emb}
    \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argsort}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{:}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{n}{k}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{bbc\PYZus{}paragraphs}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{top\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. THE GENERATOR (Gemma 2)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(\PYZdq{}Loading Generator...\PYZdq{})}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id = \PYZdq{}google/gemma\PYZhy{}2\PYZhy{}2b\PYZhy{}it\PYZdq{} }
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}tokenizer\PYZus{}gen = AutoTokenizer.from\PYZus{}pretrained(gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}model\PYZus{}gen = AutoModelForCausalLM.from\PYZus{}pretrained(}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id, }
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    torch\PYZus{}dtype=torch.bfloat16,}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    device\PYZus{}map=\PYZdq{}auto\PYZdq{}}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}).to(device)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. THE GENERATOR (Gemma 2)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Loading Generator...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{google/gemma\PYZhy{}2\PYZhy{}2b\PYZhy{}it}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} 
\PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoTokenizer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} THE SILVER BULLET FIX:}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. device\PYZus{}map=\PYZdq{}auto\PYZdq{} safely handles VRAM and prevents OOMs.}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. attn\PYZus{}implementation=\PYZdq{}eager\PYZdq{} disables PyTorch\PYZsq{}s torch.compile, }
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}    permanently preventing the FailOnRecompileLimitHit error in Jupyter!}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}gen} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{n}{gen\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{,} 
    \PY{n}{torch\PYZus{}dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bfloat16}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{device\PYZus{}map}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{auto}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{attn\PYZus{}implementation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{eager}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} 
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 4. RAG PIPELINE (Myanmar Prompt)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{rag\PYZus{}answer\PYZus{}myanmar}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step A: Retrieve context in Myanmar}
    \PY{n}{retrieved\PYZus{}docs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{retrieve\PYZus{}top\PYZus{}k}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{k}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{context\PYZus{}string} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{} }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{doc}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{doc} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{retrieved\PYZus{}docs}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step B: Create a Myanmar prompt instructing the LLM to read and extract}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} We explicitly tell it to rely ONLY on the text to prevent hallucinations}
    \PY{n}{prompt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အောက်ပါ} {\burmesefont စာသားအချက်အလက်များကို} {\burmesefont ဖော်ပြထားပါသည်။} {\burmesefont ထိုစာသားများအပေါ်} {\burmesefont အခြေခံပြီး} {\burmesefont မေးခွန်းကို} {\burmesefont မြန်မာလို} {\burmesefont ဖြေပေးပါ။} }

\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont စာသားအချက်အလက်များ}:}
\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{context\PYZus{}string}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{query}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}: }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    
    \PY{n}{inputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{prompt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{return\PYZus{}tensors}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{pt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step C: Generate}
    \PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{outputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{generate}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{inputs}\PY{p}{,} 
            \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}new\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{150}\PY{p}{,} 
            \PY{n}{pad\PYZus{}token\PYZus{}id}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eos\PYZus{}token\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{do\PYZus{}sample}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Greedy decoding for factual extraction}
        \PY{p}{)}
        
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Extract just the generated part}
    \PY{n}{answer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{outputs}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{skip\PYZus{}special\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{answer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 5. RUN THE DEMO}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} MYANMAR RAG INFERENCE \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{q1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont ဘာကြောင့်} {\burmesefont ယွမ်ငွေ} {\burmesefont သုံးသလဲ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း} {\burmesefont ၁}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{q1}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}answer\PYZus{}myanmar}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{q2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont ရှမ်းမြောက်} {\burmesefont ဘယ်မြို့တွေ} {\burmesefont မှာလဲ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း} {\burmesefont ၂}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{q2}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}answer\PYZus{}myanmar}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{q}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေလ} {\burmesefont ၂} {\burmesefont ရက်နေ့} {\burmesefont အတန်းမှာ} {\burmesefont ဘာ} {\burmesefont သင်} {\burmesefont မှာလဲ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{a}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မြန်မာစာ} {\burmesefont နဲ့} {\burmesefont ထိုင်းစာ} {\burmesefont ကို} {\burmesefont ကွန်ပျူတာ} {\burmesefont သုံးပြီး} {\burmesefont ဘာသာပြန်} {\burmesefont မယ်}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{q}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont ဆရာ} {\burmesefont က} {\burmesefont စက်ဝိုင်း} {\burmesefont နဲ့} {\burmesefont တြိဂံ} {\burmesefont ဘယ်ဟာ} {\burmesefont ကို} {\burmesefont ပိုကြိုက်} {\burmesefont သလဲ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{a}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont စက်ဝိုင်းကို} {\burmesefont ပို} {\burmesefont ကြိုက်တယ်}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{q}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မလှ} {\burmesefont က} {\burmesefont ကျောင်းပြေးဖူးလား}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{a}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont သုံးခါပဲ} {\burmesefont ပြေးဖူးပါတယ်}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. EMBEDDING THE QA PAIRS}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Embedding QA Database...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} We embed \PYZdq{}Q: ... A: ...\PYZdq{} together so the Retriever learns the mapping between them}
\PY{n}{qa\PYZus{}texts} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Q: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{q}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ A: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{a}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{item} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{qa\PYZus{}database}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{qa\PYZus{}embs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{qa\PYZus{}texts}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{convert\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}numpy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normalize\PYZus{}embeddings}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{retrieve\PYZus{}exact\PYZus{}qa}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{q\PYZus{}emb} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{convert\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}numpy}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{normalize\PYZus{}embeddings}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{scores} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{qa\PYZus{}embs} \PY{o}{@} \PY{n}{q\PYZus{}emb}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Get the index of the highest scoring match}
    \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argmax}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}score} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{scores}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{]}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Return the dictionary and the similarity score (useful for debugging)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{qa\PYZus{}database}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}idx}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}score}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. STRICT RAG PIPELINE FOR EXTRACTING ANSWERS}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{rag\PYZus{}exact\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step A: Retrieve the best matching QA pair}
    \PY{n}{best\PYZus{}match}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{score} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{retrieve\PYZus{}exact\PYZus{}qa}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step B: Create a strict prompt}
    \PY{n}{context} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Q: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}match}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{q}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{A: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{best\PYZus{}match}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{a}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
    
    \PY{n}{prompt} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont ဒါက} {\burmesefont သိထားရမည့်} {\burmesefont မေးခွန်းနဲ့} {\burmesefont အဖြေ} {\burmesefont ဖြစ်ပါတယ်။} }
\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်းက} {\burmesefont အောက်ပါ} {\burmesefont မေးခွန်းနဲ့} {\burmesefont ကိုက်ညီလျှင်} {\burmesefont အဖြေကို} {\burmesefont အဲဒီအတိုင်း} {\burmesefont ပြန်လည်ထုတ်ပေးပါ။} }
\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မမှန်ကန်လျှင်} }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မမှန်ပါ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ {\burmesefont လို့သာ} {\burmesefont ပြောပေးပါ။}}

\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont စာသားအချက်အလက်}:}
\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{context}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{query}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}

    \PY{n}{inputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{prompt}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{return\PYZus{}tensors}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{pt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Step C: Generate}
    \PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{outputs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{generate}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{inputs}\PY{p}{,} 
            \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}new\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Answers are short, we don\PYZsq{}t need 150 tokens}
            \PY{n}{pad\PYZus{}token\PYZus{}id}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eos\PYZus{}token\PYZus{}id}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{do\PYZus{}sample}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False} 
        \PY{p}{)}
        
    \PY{n}{answer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}gen}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{decode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{outputs}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{skip\PYZus{}special\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{final\PYZus{}answer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{answer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{final\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{score}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 4. RUN THE DEMO}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} EXACT QA RAG INFERENCE \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Test 1: Exact Match}
\PY{n}{q1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont ဆရာ} {\burmesefont က} {\burmesefont ဘယ်လမှာ} {\burmesefont မွေးတာလဲ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း} {\burmesefont ၁} ({\burmesefont အတိအကျကိုက်ညီ}): }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{q1}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ans1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{score1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}exact\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q1}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Retriever Score: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{score1}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ (1.0 is a perfect match)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{ans1}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Test 2: Paraphrased Match (Testing the Retriever\PYZsq{}s intelligence)}
\PY{n}{q2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont စတုဂံ} {\burmesefont ကို} {\burmesefont ပိုကြိုက်တယ်}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} 
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း} {\burmesefont ၂} ({\burmesefont အဓိပ္ပာယ်} {\burmesefont နားလည်} {\burmesefont မလည်စမ်းတာ}): }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{q2}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ans2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{score2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}exact\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q2}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Retriever Score: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{score2}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ (Lower score)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{ans2}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Test 3: Out of Domain (Testing the strict prompt)}
\PY{n}{q3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont ဘာကြောင့်} {\burmesefont ယွမ်} {\burmesefont သုံးတာလဲ}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}n}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont မေးခွန်း} {\burmesefont ၃} ({\burmesefont ဒိုမိန်း} {\burmesefont မတူတာကိုစမ်းတာ}): }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{q3}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ans3}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{score3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{rag\PYZus{}exact\PYZus{}answer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q3}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Retriever Score: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{score3}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ (Very low score)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{{\burmesefont အဖြေ}: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{ans3}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \hypertarget{the-evaluation}{%
\subsection{The Evaluation}\label{the-evaluation}}

We cannot directly compare the PPL of KenLM, LSTM, and Transformers.

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  KenLM calculates PPL per Word (e.g., predicting 1 out of 10,000
  words).
\item
  XGLM calculates PPL per Subword (e.g., breaking ``{\burmesefont မြန်မာ}'' into 3
  pieces, predicting 1 out of 256,000 pieces).
\item
  Because XGLM makes predictions more frequently (due to smaller
  pieces), its PPL mathematically looks much higher/worse, even if it's
  a better model!
\end{itemize}

\textbf{The Solution:} Bits-Per-Character (BPC). BPC normalizes
everything back to raw characters. It asks: ``How many bits of
information does the model need to guess the next single character?''

\textbf{KenLM BPC:}
\texttt{(log10\ prob\ of\ a\ word\ *\ log2(10))\ /\ number\ of\ characters\ in\ that\ word}\\
By comparing BPC, we are finally comparing Apples to Apples.

{\burmesefont ရှေ့မှာက} KenLM {\burmesefont ကို} toy {\burmesefont ဒေတာနဲ့ပဲ} {\burmesefont ဆောက်ရသေးတာမို့} KenLM {\burmesefont ကိုလည်း} myPOS corpus {\burmesefont နဲ့}
{\burmesefont အရင်ဆောက်ပါမယ်။} {\burmesefont ပြီးမှ} LSTM, Transformer {\burmesefont တို့နဲ့အတူ} {\burmesefont နှိုင်းယှဉ်ဖို့} {\burmesefont လုပ်ပါမယ်။} {\burmesefont မဟုတ်ရင်} KenLM {\burmesefont နဲ့}
{\burmesefont ဆောက်ထားတဲ့} corpus {\burmesefont က} {\burmesefont တအားသေးနေတာမို့} {\burmesefont နှိုင်းယှဉ်လို့} {\burmesefont အဆင်မပြေပါ။}

    \hypertarget{prepare-kenlm-evaluation-python-code}{%
\subsection{Prepare KenLM Evaluation Python
Code}\label{prepare-kenlm-evaluation-python-code}}

KenLM {\burmesefont မှာက} PPL {\burmesefont ကို} {\burmesefont တွက်ဖို့} commandline tool {\burmesefont အနေနဲ့} {\burmesefont ရေးမထားပါဘူး။} {\burmesefont အဲဒါကြောင့်} python
code {\burmesefont တစ်ပုဒ်ရေးလိုက်ပါတယ်။} {\burmesefont အောက်ပါအတိုင်းပါ။}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{20}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{o}{!}cat\PY{+w}{ }./kenlm/eval\PYZus{}kenlm.py
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
import kenlm, sys, math

model\_path = sys.argv[1]
test\_path = sys.argv[2]

model = kenlm.LanguageModel(model\_path)
sum\_log10 = 0.0
n\_words = 0

with open(test\_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    for line in f:
        line = line.strip()
        if not line: continue
        for prob, length, oov in model.full\_scores(line):
            sum\_log10 += prob
        n\_words += len(line.split())

\# Convert log10 to natural log, then calculate PPL
\#sum\_nats = sum\_log10 * math.log(10)
\#ppl = math.exp(-sum\_nats / n\_words) if n\_words else float("inf")
\#print(f"PPL: \{ppl:.2f\}")

\# Cleaner, unambiguous version
sum\_nats = -sum\_log10 * math.log(10)
ppl = math.exp(sum\_nats / n\_words)
entropy = sum\_nats / n\_words
print(f"PPL: \{ppl:.2f\}")
print(f"Entropy (nats): \{entropy:.4f\}")
    \end{Verbatim}

has already been used. Disabling parallelism to avoid deadlocks{\ldots}
To disable this warning, you can either:
        - Avoid using `tokenizers` before the fork if possible
        - Explicitly set the environment variable TOKENIZERS\_PARALLELISM=(true |
false)
    \end{Verbatim}

\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{math}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{json}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{pandas} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{pd}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{torch}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{pathlib} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{Path}
\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{sys}

\PY{n}{sys}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cwd}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{lstm}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{sys}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{Path}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cwd}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{transformer}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{kenlm}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{lstm\PYZus{}lm} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{TextDataset} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}Dataset}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}LM} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}Model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{Vocabulary}
\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{transformer\PYZus{}lm} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{evaluate\PYZus{}ppl} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{transformer\PYZus{}evaluate\PYZus{}ppl}

\PY{n}{device} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{cuda}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cuda}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{is\PYZus{}available}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{else} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{cpu}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Using device: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{device}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./data/otest.word.clean}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. EVALUATE KENLM (N\PYZhy{}gram)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Evaluating KenLM...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} CHANGE THIS to your new binary file!}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{kenlm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{LanguageModel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./kenlm/myanmar\PYZus{}lm.binary}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} 

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{get\PYZus{}kenlm\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
    \PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{line} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{continue}
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{prob}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{length}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{oov} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{full\PYZus{}scores}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prob}
                \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}           \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} counts \PYZlt{}/s\PYZgt{} token too}
            \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} sum\PYZus{}log10 is negative → negate once for all positive quantities}
    \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}nats}   \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}bits} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exp}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}nats} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inf}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}nats} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words}             \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inf}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{bpc\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}bits} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars}           \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inf}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bpc\PYZus{}kenlm}

\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bpc\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{get\PYZus{}kenlm\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. EVALUATE LSTM (Word\PYZhy{}level)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Evaluating LSTM...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./lstm/myanmar\PYZus{}word\PYZus{}lm.pt.vocab}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{r}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{token2idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{json}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Vocabulary}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{token2idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{token2idx}
\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{idx2token} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{k} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{k}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{token2idx}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load\PYZus{}state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./lstm/myanmar\PYZus{}word\PYZus{}lm.pt}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{map\PYZus{}location}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eval}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} The production LSTM uses sequences of length 50}
\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}ds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}Dataset}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}len}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Use the exact same loss function used during training}
\PY{n}{criterion} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{CrossEntropyLoss}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

\PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}ds}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}ds}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Add batch dimension: shape (50,) becomes (1, 50)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{unsqueeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{unsqueeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Forward pass}
        \PY{n}{out}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate loss (identical to training loop in lstm\PYZus{}lm.py)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} out shape: (1, 50, vocab\PYZus{}size)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} y shape: (1, 50)}
        \PY{n}{loss} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{criterion}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{out}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Accumulate total negative log likelihood}
        \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate final metrics}
\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exp}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. EVALUATE TRANSFORMER (XGLM)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Evaluating XGLM...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{Args}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{pass}
\PY{n}{args} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Args}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}len} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{128}
\PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stride} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{64}

\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{transformers} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{AutoTokenizer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}
\PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoTokenizer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./transformer/myanmar\PYZus{}xglm\PYZus{}word}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./transformer/myanmar\PYZus{}xglm\PYZus{}word}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} 
    \PY{n}{torch\PYZus{}dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bfloat16}\PY{p}{,} 
    \PY{n}{device\PYZus{}map}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{auto}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} 
    \PY{n}{attn\PYZus{}implementation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{eager}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}lines\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{f} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{transformer\PYZus{}evaluate\PYZus{}ppl}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}lines\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}xglm} 

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}

    \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Model}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{KenLM (Myanmar 5\PYZhy{}gram)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} 
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Test PPL}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}

    \hypertarget{flag-explanations}{%
\subsubsection{Flag explanations:}\label{flag-explanations}}

-\textbf{kndiscount}: Kneser-Ney smoothing (best general-purpose
smoothing, comparable to KenLM's default)\\
-\textbf{interpolate}: interpolates higher and lower order n-grams
(standard practice)\\
-\textbf{unk / -map-unk}: handles out-of-vocabulary words

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} SHARED METRIC FUNCTION (reused for both}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} KenLM and SRILM since both produce ARPA)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{get\PYZus{}ngram\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{    }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    Works for any kenlm\PYZhy{}loadable model (KenLM binary or SRILM ARPA).}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    Returns (ppl, entropy\PYZus{}nats, bpc).}
\PY{l+s+sd}{    \PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
    \PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{line} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{continue}
            \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{prob}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{length}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{oov} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{full\PYZus{}scores}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prob}
                \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} count \PYZlt{}/s\PYZgt{} token too}
            \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{line}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}nats}   \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}bits} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}log10} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{n}{ppl} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exp}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}nats} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inf}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ent} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sum\PYZus{}nats} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words}            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}words} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inf}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{bpc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{total\PYZus{}bits} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars}          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}chars} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{inf}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{ppl}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ent}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bpc}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. EVALUATE KENLM (N\PYZhy{}gram)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Evaluating KenLM...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{kenlm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{LanguageModel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./kenlm/myanmar\PYZus{}lm.binary}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bpc\PYZus{}kenlm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{get\PYZus{}ngram\PYZus{}metrics}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}kenlm}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. EVALUATE LSTM (Word\PYZhy{}level)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Evaluating LSTM...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./lstm/myanmar\PYZus{}word\PYZus{}lm.pt.vocab}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{r}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{token2idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{json}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Vocabulary}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{token2idx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{token2idx}
\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{idx2token} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{v}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{k} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{k}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{v} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{token2idx}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{f}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{read}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}ds}   \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{LSTM\PYZus{}Dataset}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{vocab\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}len}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{50}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{criterion} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{CrossEntropyLoss}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}

\PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{test\PYZus{}ds}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}ds}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{unsqueeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{y} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{unsqueeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{out}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}lstm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{loss} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{criterion}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{out}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{out}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{size}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{view}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum}  \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{numel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exp}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}lstm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}tokens}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 4. EVALUATE TRANSFORMER (XGLM)}
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ==========================================}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Evaluating XGLM...}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{Args}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{pass}
\PY{n}{args} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Args}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{seq\PYZus{}len} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{128}
\PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stride}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{64}

\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{transformers} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{AutoTokenizer}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}
\PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoTokenizer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./transformer/myanmar\PYZus{}xglm\PYZus{}word}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{AutoModelForCausalLM}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{from\PYZus{}pretrained}\PY{p}{(}
    \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{./transformer/myanmar\PYZus{}xglm\PYZus{}word}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{n}{torch\PYZus{}dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{bfloat16}\PY{p}{,}

    \PY{n}{attn\PYZus{}implementation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{eager}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{with} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TEST\PYZus{}FILE}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoding}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{utf\PYZhy{}8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n}{f}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}lines\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{line} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{f} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{line}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{strip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{ppl\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{transformer\PYZus{}evaluate\PYZus{}ppl}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{tokenizer\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}lines\PYZus{}xglm}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{ent\PYZus{}xglm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nll\PYZus{}xglm}

    \hypertarget{summary}{%
\subsection{Summary}\label{summary}}

{\burmesefont အခုချိန်မှာတော့} traditional {\burmesefont လို့} {\burmesefont ပြောရမယ့်} Statistical LM {\burmesefont ကနေ၊} Neural Network
based LM {\burmesefont တွေ} (LSTM, Transformer) {\burmesefont နဲ့} Large Language Model {\burmesefont တွေနဲ့တွဲသုံးတဲ့} RAG {\burmesefont အထိပါ}
{\burmesefont ဒေတာပြင်တာကနေ} {\burmesefont မော်ဒယ်ဆောက်တဲ့အပိုင်း၊} {\burmesefont ပြီးတော့} {\burmesefont ဆောက်ထားတဲ့} {\burmesefont မော်ဒယ်တွေကနေ} {\burmesefont ဘယ်လို} text
generation {\burmesefont လုပ်လို့} {\burmesefont ရသလဲ} {\burmesefont စသည်ဖြင့်} {\burmesefont အဆင့်ဆင့်} {\burmesefont လက်တွေ့လုပ်ပြခဲ့ပါတယ်။} {\burmesefont နောက်ဆုံး} {\burmesefont ဆောက်ထားတာမတူညီကြတဲ့} LM
{\burmesefont တွေအကြား} {\burmesefont မှာ} Bits-Per-Character (BPC) {\burmesefont နဲ့} {\burmesefont ပြန်ညှိပြီး} evaluation {\burmesefont လုပ်တာကိုလည်း}
{\burmesefont သင်ကြားပေးခဲ့ပါတယ်။}

{\burmesefont ဆရာ} {\burmesefont ပြောရဲပါတယ်။} LM {\burmesefont နဲ့ပတ်သက်ပြီး} {\burmesefont ဒီလောက်စုံအောင်} {\burmesefont လက်တွေ့လုပ်ပြထားတဲ့} Notebook {\burmesefont က} {\burmesefont ရှားပါလိမ့်မယ်။}
{\burmesefont လုပ်ပြထားတဲ့} {\burmesefont အဆင့်တွေအားလုံးကို} {\burmesefont ဒေတာကိုပြောင်းလိုက်ပြီး} {\burmesefont ကိုယ်တိုင်} {\burmesefont အစအဆုံး} {\burmesefont ပြီးအောင်} run {\burmesefont ကြည့်ရင်းနဲ့}
{\burmesefont ကြိုးစားလေ့လာသွားကြပါလို့။}
